management is implemented through a multi-layered architecture combining process supervision, gRPC client communication, health checking, and automatic crash recovery.\\n\\n## Process Supervisor and Lifecycle Management\\n\\nThe core process supervisor is implemented in `pkg/plugins/manager/process/process.go`. The `Service` struct (ProvideService) manages the complete lifecycle of backend plugins:\\n\\n- **Start method**: Initiates plugin processes for managed backend plugins and launches automatic crash recovery via `startPluginAndKeepItAlive`\\n- **keepPluginAlive function**: Implements the restart policy by continuously monitoring plugin processes using a ticker (default 1-second intervals). When a plugin crashes (detected via `p.Exited()`), it automatically restarts the process using `p.Start(context.Background())`\\n- **Stop method**: Gracefully terminates plugin processes by calling `p.Decommission()` and `p.Stop(ctx)`\\n\\nThe `Manager` interface in `pkg/plugins/manager/process/ifaces.go` defines the contract with Start and Stop methods.\\n\\n## gRPC Client Connection\\n\\ngRPC communication to backend plugins is handled through multiple coordinated components:\\n\\n**grpc_plugin.go**: The `grpcPlugin` struct implements the `backendplugin.Plugin` interface:\\n- Uses `hashicorp/go-plugin` with gRPC protocol version negotiation\\n- Maintains connection state with pluginState enum (NotStarted, StartInit, StartSuccess, StartFail, Stopped)\\n- The `Start` method creates a new plugin.Client and negotiates protocol version\\n- The `Stop` method kills the client process via `p.client.Kill()`\\n- The `getPluginClient` method checks if the client is alive and ready\\n\\n**client.go**: Provides factory functions and configuration:\\n- `NewBackendPlugin` creates managed plugin factories\\n- `newClientConfig` builds go-plugin ClientConfig with gRPC handshake, versioned plugins, and environment variables\\n- Supports both process mode and container mode execution\\n- Integrates OpenTelemetry tracing via `otelgrpc.NewClientHandler`\\n\\n**client_v2.go**: The `ClientV2` struct aggregates gRPC service clients:\\n- Combines DiagnosticsClient, ResourceClient, DataClient, StreamClient, AdmissionClient, ConversionClient, and RendererPlugin\\n- `newClientV2` dispenses and wraps individual gRPC clients from the plugin connection\\n\\n**client_proto.go**: The `ProtoClient` interface provides the high-level gRPC client abstraction:\\n- Wraps the internal `grpcPlugin` for external consumption\\n- Methods like QueryData, CallResource, CheckHealth delegate to underlying ClientV2 implementations\\n\\n## Health Check Implementation\\n\\nHealth checking is integrated throughout the gRPC layer:\\n\\n- **grpcPlugin.CheckHealth**: Routes health check requests through `getPluginClient` to ensure plugin availability\\n- **ClientV2.CheckHealth**: Implements the actual gRPC health check call to the plugin's DiagnosticsClient\\n  - Handles Unimplemented status gracefully (returns HealthStatusUnknown)\\n  - Converts between backend.CheckHealthRequest and pluginv2 protobuf messages\\n  - Returns error if plugin client is unavailable\\n\\n## Plugin Restart Policy on Crash\\n\\nThe crash recovery system is sophisticated:\\n\\n1. **Automatic Detection**: `keepPluginAlive` continuously polls via ticker, detecting crashed processes through `p.Exited()`\\n2. **Non-Core Plugin Only**: Core plugins are excluded from restart monitoring (checked in `startPluginAndKeepItAlive`)\\n3. **Graceful Restart**: On crash detection, the system logs the event and attempts restart via `p.Start(context.Background())`\\n4. **Error Handling**: If restart fails, the error is logged but the monitoring continues trying in future ticks\\n5. **Graceful Shutdown**: Decommissioned plugins are detected and monitoring stops automatically\\n\\n## Initialization and Termination Pipeline\\n\\n**initialization/steps.go**: \\n- `BackendClientInit.Initialize`: Registers backend plugin clients using `BackendFactoryProvider`\\n- `BackendClientStarter.Start`: Invokes the process manager to start the backend plugin process\\n\\n**termination/steps.go**:\\n- `BackendProcessTerminator.Terminate`: Delegates to process.Manager.Stop for clean shutdown\\n- `Deregister.Deregister`: Removes plugins from the registry after termination\\n\\nThe backend plugin system in Grafana provides resilient, self-healing plugin process management with automatic crash recovery, gRPC-based inter-process communication, and integrated health checking.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":951,"cache_read_input_tokens":88017,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":951},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"157416e5-a7cf-4258-9a35-a7fc361b3398","uuid":"b18c84f0-2dbb-4acb-9193-3b86dfe01b8c"}
